Recommended Import Approach
- Prefer JSON as the source of truth. Start with files that have captions/timestamps/media paths, especially any under paths like content, posts, media, or your_instagram_activity.
- Resolve Instagram media URI/path values relative to the export root; do not assume they are site-ready URLs.
- Treat media or attachments arrays with more than one item as carousel candidates.
- Preserve original creation timestamps and convert them later into Jekyll post/gallery dates.
- Keep this discovery phase read-only for media. Copying, thumbnailing, uploads, and Jekyll item creation should happen in a separate import script after the structure is confirmed.
